 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.02. Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&#160;23, 2021, we increased the size of the Mondel&#275;z International Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) from 12 to 13 members and appointed Ertharin Cousin to the Board, effective January&#160;1, 2022. The Board has not yet determined to which committees it will appoint Ms.&#160;Cousin. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ms.&#160;Cousin will receive the same compensation and indemnification as our other <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-employee</span> directors. The compensation program is described in our Proxy Statement on Schedule 14A filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;) on April&#160;7, 2021. The form of indemnification agreement is an exhibit to our Annual Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> filed with the SEC on February&#160;5, 2021. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">There are no transactions between Ms.&#160;Cousin and us that would be reportable under Item 404(a) of Regulation <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-K.</span> Ms.&#160;Cousin was not selected pursuant to any arrangement or understanding between her and any other person. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A copy of our press release regarding these events is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01. </TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Appoints Ertharin Cousin </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>to Board of Directors </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CHICAGO, Nov. 29, 2021 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) today announced the appointment of Ertharin
Cousin, Founder, President and CEO of the Food Systems of the Future Institute, to the Company&#146;s Board of Directors, effective January&nbsp;1, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We welcome Ertharin to our Board and look forward to benefitting from her wealth of knowledge and expertise,&#148; said Dirk Van de Put,
Chairman&nbsp;&amp; CEO of Mondel&#275;z International. &#147;Her expert perspective on food policy and sustainability issues will bring important insights and value to our Board and team as we continue advancing our strategy and ESG priorities as a
global snacking leader.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cousin possesses more than 30 years of experience in the worldwide food industry, working in the
government, nonprofit and corporate sectors. Her experience includes serving as Executive Director of the United Nations World Food Programme; Ambassador and Permanent Representative to United Nations Food and Agriculture Agencies in the Obama
Administration; Executive Vice President and Chief Operating Officer of America&#146;s Second Harvest; and Senior Vice President for Public Affairs at Albertsons Companies Inc. She currently serves on the Board of Directors of Bayer AG. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cousin&#146;s appointment expands the size of the Company&#146;s Board of Directors to 13 members. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g323481dsp1.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2020 net revenues
of approximately $27&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>OREO</I>, <I>belVita </I>and <I>LU </I>biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk</I>, <I>Milka </I>and <I>Toblerone </I>chocolate; <I>Sour
Patch Kids </I>candy and <I>Trident </I>gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit www.mondelezinternational.com or follow the company on Twitter at
www.twitter.com/MDLZ . </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">### </P>
